    -v, --verbose         be verbose

    -i, --interactive     interactive picking
    -p, --patch           select hunks interactively
    -e, --edit            edit current diff and apply
    -f, --force           allow adding otherwise ignored files
    -u, --update          update tracked files
    --renormalize         renormalize EOL of tracked files (implies -u)
    -N, --intent-to-add   record only the fact that the path will be added later
    -A, --all             add changes from all tracked and untracked files
    --ignore-removal      ignore paths removed in the working tree (same as --no-all)
    --refresh             don't add, only refresh the index
    --ignore-errors       just skip files which cannot be added because of errors
    --ignore-missing      check if - even missing - files are ignored in dry run
    --chmod (+|-)x        override the executable bit of the listed files
    --pathspec-from-file <file>

## Evidence Mode — Blast Radius of `fanout.Querier`

---

### Current State: The Call Chain

**`fanout.Querier()`** at `storage/fanout.go:74` is the method on the unexported `fanout` struct. It:
1. Calls `f.primary.Querier()` (TSDB/readyStorage) — **VERIFIED** (`fanout.go:75`)
2. Calls each `f.secondaries[x].Querier()` (remote storage) — **VERIFIED** (`fanout.go:82`)
3. Wraps results in `NewMergeQuerier(primary_queriers, secondaries, ChainedSeriesMerge)` — **VERIFIED** (`fanout.go:98`)

**Single instantiation** at `cmd/prometheus/main.go:896`:
```go
fanoutStorage = storage.NewFanout(logger, localStorage, remoteStorage)
```
— **VERIFIED** (no other callers exist in non-test code)

This `fanoutStorage` is wired into 3 subsystems:

| Subsystem | main.go line | Role |
|-----------|--------------|------|
| Web Handler | `1013` | `cfg.web.Storage = fanoutStorage` → becomes `api.Queryable` |

| Scrape Manager | `944` | `nil, fanoutStorage` — uses Appender, **NOT** Querier |

**VERIFIED** (lines cross-referenced with `web/web.go`, `rules/manager.go`)

### Historical Context / Secondary Consumers

The `Querier` returned by `fanout.Querier()` is always a `mergeGenericQuerier` (via `querierAdapter`). Its methods fan out to all primary + secondary queriers:

- **`Select()`** — `storage/merge.go:132` — concurrent/sequential select across all sub-queriers, merged via `ChainedSeriesMerge` — **VERIFIED**
- **`LabelValues()`** — `storage/merge.go:194` — merged via `mergeResults` — **VERIFIED**
- **`LabelNames()`** — `storage/merge.go:260` — merged via `mergeResults` — **VERIFIED**
- **`Close()`** — `storage/merge.go:271` — closes all sub-queriers — **VERIFIED**

Tests at `storage/fanout_test.go:77,182,265` verify the method directly — **VERIFIED**.
